Easy and Fun to Play</h2>
<p>Casual games aren’t complicated, making them perfect for a quick game in your web browser. You can load into a casual game instantly solo or <a target="_blank" href="https://www.crazygames.com/t/2-player">2-player</a>, no need to download, and you’ll know how to play it within minutes. Most casual games are free-to-play, like all the games on CrazyGames.</p>
<p>Some of our best casual games include <a target="_blank" href="https://www.crazygames.com/game/geometry-dash-online">Geometry Dash</a> and <a target="_blank" href="https://www.crazygames.com/game/drift-boss">Drift Boss</a>. Both of these titles feature fast-paced arcade-style gameplay without being complicated. There’s also <a target="_blank" href="https://www.crazygames.com/t/classic">classic games</a> that deserve a mention for pioneering the casual style like <a target="_blank" href="https://www.crazygames.com/game/bubble-shooter-classic">Bubble Shooter</a>.</p>
<h3>Hyper-Casual Games - The Easiest</h3>
<p>Hyper-casual games take the casual genre one step further with instant playability. It generally takes less than a minute to learn how to play a hyper-casual game due to the single game mechanic and simple controls, often being only <a target="_blank" href="https://www.crazygames.com/t/one-button">one button</a> like <a target="_blank" href="https://www.crazygames.com/game/slice-master">Slice Master</a>.</p>
<p>The hyper-casual genre emerged on mobile, but it suits the web even better, as they don’t take long to load, and there’s no download required. Check out some hyper-casual <a target="_blank" href="https://www.crazygames.com/t/mini">minigames</a>.</p>
<p>Newer games in this space include <a target="_blank" href="https://www.crazygames.com/game/eggy-car">Eggy Car</a> and <a target="_blank" href="https://www.crazygames.com/game/tiny-fishing">Tiny Fishing</a>.</p>
<h3>Match 3 Casual Games</h3>
<p><a target="_blank" href="https://www.crazygames.com/t/match-3">Match 3 </a>games like <a target="_blank" href="https://www.crazygames.com/game/tile-guru">Tile Guru</a> and <a target="_blank" href="https://www.crazygames.com/game/piles-of-mahjong-jhb">Piles of Mahjong</a> can be quite addictive. Browse our <a target="_blank" href="https://www.crazygames.com/t/mahjong">Mahjong games</a> for even more of the same. Merge games offer a similar gameplay, and some of our most popular games worth trying, include <a target="_blank" href="https://www.crazygames.com/game/little-alchemy">Little Alchemy</a>, <a target="_blank" href="https://www.crazygames.com/game/little-alchemy-2">Little Alchemy 2</a>, and <a target="_blank" href="https://www.crazygames.com/game/designville-merge-design">Designville Merge &amp; Design</a>.</p>
<h3>The Best Casual Games. These are Addictive!</h3>
<p>The best casual games take hyper-casual games one step further with just enough magic formula to make them super addictive! You could easily sink hours into games like <a target="_blank" href="https://www.crazygames.com/game/happy-wheels">Happy Wheels</a> and <a target="_blank" href="https://www.crazygames.com/game/bloons-tower-defense">Bloons Tower Defense</a>, which are simple games with more progression than the average casual game to keep you hooked.</p>
<p><a target="_blank" href="https://www.crazygames.com/game/super-auto-pets">Super Auto Pets</a> are also really engaging games to dip into for a quick gaming session!</p>
<h3>Fun and Challenging Casual Games</h3>
<p><a target="_blank" href="https://www.crazygames.com/game/papas-pizzeria">Papa's Pizz</a>eria, where you get to serve up slices to hungry customers. <a target="_blank" href="https://www.crazygames.com/game/friday-night-funkin">Friday Night Funkin</a> is a musical rhythm game where you compete in freestyle music battles. <a target="_blank" href="https://www.crazygames.com/game/blob-opera">Blob Opera</a> is a game that uses a machine learning model trained on real voices to make it easy for anyone to create amazing operatic music.</p>
<h3>Why Play Casual?</h3>
<p>If you don’t have the patience or time to learn the ins and outs of a complex<a target="_blank" href="https://www.crazygames.com/t/strategy"> strategy </a>or <a target="_blank" href="https://www.crazygames.com/t/rpg">RPG game</a>, then free casual games are probably ideal for you.
